     2→ * Document Type Registry Composable
     3→ *
     4→ * Manages the registry of supported document types and the currently active
     5→ * document type. Each document type bundles its own parser, validator,
     6→ * available templates, and sample XML path.
     7→ *
     8→ * Architecture note: this composable is the single source of truth for

    11→ */
    12→
    13→import { computed, onMounted } from 'vue'
    14→import { parseXml as parseCoverLetterXml, validateXml as validateCoverLetterXml } from '~/composables/useXmlParser'

    16→
    17→const LS_KEY = 'ohmydoc_document_type'
    18→
    19→// ─── Public interfaces ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    20→
    21→export interface DocumentTypeConfig {
    22→  /** Internal key used in URLs, localStorage, and template associations */
    23→  name: string
    24→  /** Human-readable label shown in the UI */
    25→  displayName: string
    26→  /** Short description of the document type */
    27→  description: string
    28→  /** Path to the bundled sample XML (relative to /public) */
    29→  sampleXmlPath: string
    30→  /** Template to activate when this document type is first selected */
    31→  defaultTemplate: string
    32→  /** Names of templates registered in useTemplate that support this type */
    33→  templates: string[]
    34→  /** Parse an XML string into a typed data object for template rendering */
    35→  parse: (xmlString: string) => ParseResult
    36→  /** Validate well-formedness and schema requirements without full parsing */
    37→  validate: (xmlString: string) => ValidationResult
    38→}
    39→
    40→// ─── Registry ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    41→
    42→/**
    43→ * All registered document types.
    44→ *
    45→ * To add a new type, append an entry here following the same shape as
    46→ * 'cover-letter'. The parser and validator functions live in their own
    47→ * composable (e.g. useResumParser.ts) and are imported at the top of this file.
    48→ */
    49→const documentTypes: Record<string, DocumentTypeConfig> = {
    50→  'cover-letter': {
    51→    name: 'cover-letter',
    52→    displayName: 'Cover Letter',
    53→    description: 'Professional cover letter for job applications',
    54→    sampleXmlPath: '/samples/cover-letter.xml',
    55→    defaultTemplate: 'modern',
    56→    templates: ['modern', 'classic', 'minimal'],
    57→    parse: parseCoverLetterXml,
    58→    validate: validateCoverLetterXml,
    59→  },
    60→}
    61→
    62→// ─── Composable ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    63→
    64→/**
    65→ * Reactive document type selection.
    66→ *
    67→ * State is shared across all component instances via useState and persisted
    68→ * to localStorage so the selection survives page reloads.
    69→ */
    70→export function useDocumentType() {
    71→  const activeDocumentType = useState<string>('activeDocumentType', () => 'cover-letter')
    72→
    73→  // Restore from localStorage after hydration (client-only)
    74→  onMounted(() => {
    75→    try {
    76→      const saved = localStorage.getItem(LS_KEY)
    77→      if (saved && documentTypes[saved]) {
    78→        activeDocumentType.value = saved
    79→      }
    80→    }
    81→    catch {
    82→      // Ignore storage errors (private browsing, quota exceeded, etc.)
    83→    }
    84→  })
    85→
    86→  /**
    87→   * Switch to a different document type and persist the choice to localStorage.
    88→   * Also resets the active template to that type's default.
    89→   */
    90→  function setActiveDocumentType(name: string) {
    91→    if (!documentTypes[name]) {
    92→      console.warn(`Document type "${name}" not found. Available: ${Object.keys(documentTypes).join(', ')}`)
    93→      return
    94→    }
    95→    activeDocumentType.value = name
    96→    try {
    97→      localStorage.setItem(LS_KEY, name)
    98→    }
    99→    catch {
   100→      // Ignore storage errors
   101→    }
   102→  }
   103→
   104→  /** Config object for the currently active document type */
   105→  const currentDocumentType = computed<DocumentTypeConfig | undefined>(
   106→    () => documentTypes[activeDocumentType.value],
   107→  )
   108→
   109→  /** All registered document type config objects */
   110→  function getAvailableDocumentTypes(): DocumentTypeConfig[] {
   111→    return Object.values(documentTypes)
   112→  }
   113→
   114→  return {
   115→    activeDocumentType,
   116→    currentDocumentType,
   117→    setActiveDocumentType,
   118→    getAvailableDocumentTypes,
   119→  }
   120→}

USERMESSAGE #10
✓ TOOL RESULT
SUCCESS 
     1→/**
     2→ * Template System Composable
     3→ *
     4→ * Provides reactive template selection and management for document rendering.
     5→ * Active template is shared across all components via useState and persisted
     6→ * to localStorage so the selection survives page reloads.
     7→ */
     8→
     9→import { onMounted, computed } from 'vue'
    10→import type { Component } from 'vue'
    11→import CoverLetterModern from '~/templates/modern/CoverLetterModern.vue'
    12→import CoverLetterClassic from '~/templates/classic/CoverLetterClassic.vue'
    13→import CoverLetterMinimal from '~/templates/minimal/CoverLetterMinimal.vue'
    14→
    15→const LS_KEY = 'ohmydoc_template'
    16→
    17→// Template metadata interface
    18→export interface TemplateMetadata {
    19→  name: string
    20→  displayName: string
    21→  description: string
    22→  /** Document type names this template supports (matches DocumentTypeConfig.name) */
    23→  documentTypes: string[]
    24→}
    25→
    26→// Template registry type
    27→export interface TemplateRegistry {
    28→  [key: string]: {
    29→    component: Component
    30→    metadata: TemplateMetadata
    31→  }
    32→}
    33→
    34→/**
    35→ * Template Registry
    36→ *
    37→ * Maps template names to their Vue components and metadata.
    38→ * All templates use the same ParsedData props interface for consistency.
    39→ */
    40→const templates: TemplateRegistry = {
    41→  modern: {
    42→    component: CoverLetterModern,
    43→    metadata: {
    44→      name: 'modern',
    45→      displayName: 'Modern',
    46→      description: 'Professional cover letter template with modern styling and clean typography',
    47→      documentTypes: ['cover-letter'],
    48→    },
    49→  },
    50→  classic: {
    51→    component: CoverLetterClassic,
    52→    metadata: {
    53→      name: 'classic',
    54→      displayName: 'Classic',
    55→      description: 'Traditional cover letter with table-based layout and formal styling',
    56→      documentTypes: ['cover-letter'],
    57→    },
    58→  },
    59→  minimal: {
    60→    component: CoverLetterMinimal,
    61→    metadata: {
    62→      name: 'minimal',
    63→      displayName: 'Minimal',
    64→      description: 'Clean, minimalist cover letter design with simple structure and generous whitespace',
    65→      documentTypes: ['cover-letter'],
    66→    },
    67→  },
    68→}
    69→
    70→/**
    71→ * Composable function to use the reactive template system in Vue components.
    72→ *
    73→ * Active template state is shared across all component instances via useState.
    74→ * On mount, the saved localStorage value is restored (client-side only).
    75→ *
    76→ * @returns Reactive template state and control functions
    77→ */
    78→export function useTemplate() {
    79→  // Shared reactive state — useState ensures all components see the same value
    80→  const activeTemplate = useState<string>('activeTemplate', () => 'modern')
    81→
    82→  // Restore from localStorage after hydration (client-only, runs once per component mount)
    83→  onMounted(() => {
    84→    try {
    85→      const saved = localStorage.getItem(LS_KEY)
    86→      if (saved && templates[saved]) {
    87→        activeTemplate.value = saved
    88→      }
    89→    }
    90→    catch {
    91→      // Ignore storage errors (private browsing, quota exceeded, etc.)
    92→    }
    93→  })
    94→
    95→  /**
    96→   * Switch to a different template and persist the choice to localStorage.
    97→   */
    98→  function setActiveTemplate(name: string) {
    99→    if (!templates[name]) {
   100→      console.warn(`Template "${name}" not found. Available: ${Object.keys(templates).join(', ')}`)
   101→      return
   102→    }
   103→    activeTemplate.value = name
   104→    try {
   105→      localStorage.setItem(LS_KEY, name)
   106→    }
   107→    catch {
   108→      // Ignore storage errors
   109→    }
   110→  }
   111→
   112→  /** Reactive component for the currently active template */
   113→  const currentTemplate = computed<Component | undefined>(
   114→    () => templates[activeTemplate.value]?.component,
   115→  )
   116→
   117→  /** Metadata for the currently active template */
   118→  const currentTemplateMetadata = computed<TemplateMetadata | undefined>(
   119→    () => templates[activeTemplate.value]?.metadata,
   120→  )
   121→
   122→  /** Names of all registered templates */
   123→  function getAvailableTemplates(): string[] {
   124→    return Object.keys(templates)
   125→  }
   126→
   127→  /** Metadata objects for all registered templates */
   128→  function getAllTemplateMetadata(): TemplateMetadata[] {
   129→    return Object.values(templates).map(t => t.metadata)
   130→  }
   131→
   132→  /** Metadata objects for templates that support the given document type */
   133→  function getTemplatesForDocumentType(docType: string): TemplateMetadata[] {
   134→    return Object.values(templates)
   135→      .filter(t => t.metadata.documentTypes.includes(docType))
   136→      .map(t => t.metadata)
   137→  }
   138→
   139→  return {
   140→    activeTemplate,
   141→    setActiveTemplate,
   142→    currentTemplate,

     1→/**
     2→ * XML Parser Composable
     3→ *
     4→ * Provides XML parsing functionality using browser's native DOMParser API.
     5→ * Zero dependencies approach for fast, simple XML parsing (DECISIONS.md Decision 6).
     6→ */
     7→
     8→// TypeScript interfaces matching the XML schema from docs/sample/cover-letter.xml
     9→
    10→export interface Address {
    11→  street: string
    12→  city: string
    13→  state: string
    14→  zipCode: string
    15→}
    16→
    17→export interface ContactInformation {
    18→  phone: string
    19→  email: string
    20→}
    21→
    22→export interface Applicant {
    23→  name: string
    24→  address: Address
    25→  contactInformation: ContactInformation
    26→}

    28→export interface Achievement {
    29→  text: string
    30→}
    31→
    32→export interface Experience {
    33→  employer: string
    34→  achievements: Achievement[]
    35→}
    36→
    37→export interface Letter {
    38→  salutation: string
    39→  introduction: string
    40→  experienceSection: Experience[]
    41→  motivation: string
    42→  closing: string
    43→  signature: string
    44→}

    48→  company: string
    49→  address: Address
    50→}

    52→export interface ParsedData {
    53→  formatStyle?: string
    54→  applicant: Applicant
    55→  date: string
    56→  recipient: Recipient
    57→  letter: Letter
    58→}
    59→
    60→export interface ValidationResult {
    61→  isValid: boolean
    62→  error?: string
    63→}
    64→
    65→export interface ParseResult {
    66→  success: boolean
    67→  data?: ParsedData
    68→  error?: string
    69→}
    70→
    71→/**
    72→ * Helper function to safely extract text content from an XML element
    73→ */
    74→function getTextContent(element: Element | null, tagName: string, parentName: string = 'document'): string {
    75→  if (!element) {
    76→    throw new Error(`Missing required element: ${tagName} in ${parentName}`)
    77→  }
    78→  const node = element.querySelector(tagName)
    79→  if (!node) {
    80→    throw new Error(`Missing required element: ${tagName} in ${parentName}`)
    81→  }
    82→  return node.textContent?.trim() || ''
    83→}
    84→
    85→/**
    86→ * Parse address element (reusable for applicant and recipient addresses)
    87→ */
    88→function parseAddress(addressElement: Element | null, context: string): Address {
    89→  if (!addressElement) {
    90→    throw new Error(`Missing address element in ${context}`)
    91→  }
    92→
    93→  return {
    94→    street: getTextContent(addressElement, 'street', `${context} address`),
    95→    city: getTextContent(addressElement, 'city', `${context} address`),
    96→    state: getTextContent(addressElement, 'state', `${context} address`),
    97→    zipCode: getTextContent(addressElement, 'zipCode', `${context} address`),
    98→  }
    99→}
   100→
   101→/**
   102→ * Validate XML for well-formedness and basic schema requirements
   103→ *
   104→ * @param xmlString - XML string to validate
   105→ * @returns ValidationResult with isValid flag and optional error message
   106→ */
   107→export function validateXml(xmlString: string): ValidationResult {
   108→  if (!xmlString || xmlString.trim() === '') {
   109→    return {
   110→      isValid: false,
   111→      error: 'XML input is empty. Please provide valid XML content.',
   112→    }
   113→  }
   114→
   115→  const parser = new DOMParser()
   116→  const xmlDoc = parser.parseFromString(xmlString, 'text/xml')
   117→
   118→  // Check for parser errors
   119→  const parserError = xmlDoc.querySelector('parsererror')
   120→  if (parserError) {
   121→    // Extract meaningful error message from parsererror element
   122→    const errorText = parserError.textContent || 'Unknown XML parsing error'
   123→
   124→    // Provide user-friendly error messages for common issues
   125→    if (errorText.includes('unclosed tag') || errorText.includes('Opening and ending tag mismatch')) {
   126→      return {
   127→        isValid: false,
   128→        error: 'XML has unclosed or mismatched tags. Please check that all opening tags have corresponding closing tags.',
   129→      }
   130→    }
   131→    if (errorText.includes('Unexpected end of file') || errorText.includes('premature end of data')) {
   132→      return {
   133→        isValid: false,
   134→        error: 'XML is incomplete. The document appears to end unexpectedly.',
   135→      }
   136→    }
   137→    if (errorText.includes('invalid character') || errorText.includes('not well-formed')) {
   138→      return {
   139→        isValid: false,
   140→        error: 'XML contains invalid characters or syntax. Please check for special characters that need to be escaped.',
   141→      }
   142→    }
   143→
   144→    return {
   145→      isValid: false,
   146→      error: `XML parsing error: ${errorText}`,
   147→    }
   148→  }
   149→
   150→  // Check for root element
   151→  const root = xmlDoc.documentElement
   152→  if (!root || root.tagName !== 'applicationDocument') {
   153→    return {
   154→      isValid: false,
   155→      error: 'Invalid XML structure. Root element must be <applicationDocument>.',
   156→    }
   157→  }
   158→
   159→  // Check for required top-level elements
   160→  const requiredElements = ['applicant', 'date', 'recipient', 'letter']
   161→  for (const elementName of requiredElements) {
   162→    if (!root.querySelector(elementName)) {
   163→      return {
   164→        isValid: false,
   165→        error: `Missing required element: <${elementName}>. All application documents must include applicant, date, recipient, and letter sections.`,
   166→      }
   167→    }
   168→  }
   169→
   170→  return { isValid: true }
   171→}
   172→
   173→/**
   174→ * Parse XML string into structured data object
   175→ *
   176→ * @param xmlString - XML string to parse
   177→ * @returns ParseResult with success flag, parsed data, or error message
   178→ */
   179→export function parseXml(xmlString: string): ParseResult {
   180→  try {
   181→    // First validate the XML
   182→    const validation = validateXml(xmlString)
   183→    if (!validation.isValid) {
   184→      return {
   185→        success: false,
   186→        error: validation.error,
   187→      }
   188→    }
   189→
   190→    const parser = new DOMParser()
   191→    const xmlDoc = parser.parseFromString(xmlString, 'text/xml')
   192→    const root = xmlDoc.documentElement
   193→
   194→    // Extract formatStyle attribute (optional)
   195→    const formatStyle = root.getAttribute('formatStyle') || undefined
   196→
   197→    // Parse applicant section
   198→    const applicantElement = root.querySelector('applicant')
   199→    if (!applicantElement) {
   200→      throw new Error('Missing required element: applicant')
   201→    }
   202→
   203→    const applicant: Applicant = {
   204→      name: getTextContent(applicantElement, 'name', 'applicant'),
   205→      address: parseAddress(applicantElement.querySelector('address'), 'applicant'),
   206→      contactInformation: {
   207→        phone: getTextContent(applicantElement, 'contactInformation phone', 'applicant'),
   208→        email: getTextContent(applicantElement, 'contactInformation email', 'applicant'),
   209→      },
   210→    }
   211→
   212→    // Parse date
   213→    const date = getTextContent(root, 'date')
   214→
   215→    // Parse recipient section
   216→    const recipientElement = root.querySelector('recipient')
   217→    if (!recipientElement) {
   218→      throw new Error('Missing required element: recipient')
   219→    }
   220→
   221→    const recipient: Recipient = {
   222→      position: getTextContent(recipientElement, 'position', 'recipient'),
   223→      company: getTextContent(recipientElement, 'company', 'recipient'),
   224→      address: parseAddress(recipientElement.querySelector('address'), 'recipient'),
   225→    }
   226→
   227→    // Parse letter section
   228→    const letterElement = root.querySelector('letter')
   229→    if (!letterElement) {
   230→      throw new Error('Missing required element: letter')
   231→    }
   232→
   233→    // Parse experiences
   234→    const experienceElements = letterElement.querySelectorAll('experienceSection experience')
   235→    const experiences: Experience[] = Array.from(experienceElements).map((expElement) => {
   236→      const employer = expElement.querySelector('employer')?.textContent?.trim() || ''
   237→      const achievementElements = expElement.querySelectorAll('achievements achievement')
   238→      const achievements: Achievement[] = Array.from(achievementElements).map(ach => ({
   239→        text: ach.textContent?.trim() || '',
   240→      }))
   241→
   242→      return {
   243→        employer,
   244→        achievements,
   245→      }
   246→    })
   247→
   248→    const letter: Letter = {
   249→      salutation: getTextContent(letterElement, 'salutation', 'letter'),
   250→      introduction: getTextContent(letterElement, 'introduction', 'letter'),
   251→      experienceSection: experiences,
   252→      motivation: getTextContent(letterElement, 'motivation', 'letter'),
   253→      closing: getTextContent(letterElement, 'closing', 'letter'),
   254→      signature: getTextContent(letterElement, 'signature', 'letter'),
   255→    }
   256→
   257→    const parsedData: ParsedData = {
   258→      formatStyle,
   259→      applicant,
   260→      date,
   261→      recipient,
   262→      letter,
   263→    }
   264→
   265→    return {
   266→      success: true,
   267→      data: parsedData,
   268→    }
   269→  }
   270→  catch (error) {
   271→    const errorMessage = error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error occurred during parsing'
   272→    return {
   273→      success: false,
   274→      error: `Failed to parse XML: ${errorMessage}`,
   275→    }
   276→  }
   277→}
   278→
   279→/**
   280→ * Composable function to use XML parser in Vue components
   281→ */
   282→export function useXmlParser() {
   283→  return {
   284→    parseXml,
   285→    validateXml,
   286→  }
   287→}

    68→<script setup lang="ts">
    69→import { ref, watch, onMounted, onUnmounted } from 'vue'
    70→import { useDocumentType } from '~/composables/useDocumentType'
    71→
    72→/**
    73→ * Main Application Page - MVP 6: Dual-Panel Integration
    74→ *
    75→ * Features:
    76→ * - Welcome screen on first load (no saved data in localStorage)
    77→ * - Dual-panel 50/50 layout (CSS Grid)
    78→ * - 300ms debounced real-time updates (per DECISIONS.md)
    79→ * - Persists XML content to localStorage
    80→ * - Minimum 1024px responsive design
    81→ * - Document type switching loads the appropriate sample XML
    82→ */
    83→
    84→const LS_KEY = 'ohmydoc_xml_content'
    85→
    86→const { activeDocumentType, currentDocumentType } = useDocumentType()
    87→
    88→// Set page metadata
    89→useHead({
    90→  title: 'OhMyDoc - XML to HTML Transformer',
    91→})
    92→
    93→// Welcome screen is shown when no saved data exists
    94→const showWelcome = ref(true)
    95→const isSampleLoading = ref(false)
    96→
    97→// Reactive state for XML content
    98→const xmlContent = ref('')
    99→const debouncedXmlContent = ref('')
   100→
   101→// Debounce timer ref
   102→let debounceTimer: ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null = null
   103→
   104→/**
   105→ * Debounce watcher: Updates preview 300ms after user stops typing
   106→ * Per DECISIONS.md Decision 5: 300ms < 500ms threshold provides smooth UX
   107→ * without feeling laggy or causing excessive re-parsing
   108→ */
   109→watch(xmlContent, (newValue) => {
   110→  if (debounceTimer) {
   111→    clearTimeout(debounceTimer)
   112→  }
   113→
   114→  debounceTimer = setTimeout(() => {
   115→    debouncedXmlContent.value = newValue
   116→    // Persist to localStorage so returning users skip the welcome screen
   117→    try {
   118→      localStorage.setItem(LS_KEY, newValue)
   119→    }
   120→    catch {
   121→      // Ignore storage errors (private browsing, quota exceeded, etc.)
   122→    }
   123→  }, 300)
   124→})
   125→
   126→/**
   127→ * Fetch and apply the sample XML for the active document type.
   128→ * Called by the "Start with a sample" button and when switching document types.
   129→ */
   130→async function loadSample() {
   131→  isSampleLoading.value = true
   132→  const samplePath = currentDocumentType.value?.sampleXmlPath ?? '/samples/cover-letter.xml'
   133→  try {
   134→    const response = await fetch(samplePath)
   135→    if (!response.ok) {
   136→      throw new Error(`HTTP ${response.status}`)
   137→    }
   138→    const sampleXml = await response.text()
   139→    xmlContent.value = sampleXml
   140→    debouncedXmlContent.value = sampleXml
   141→    showWelcome.value = false
   142→  }
   143→  catch (error) {
   144→    console.error('Error loading sample XML:', error)
   145→    // Still dismiss welcome and show an empty editor rather than getting stuck
   146→    showWelcome.value = false
   147→  }
   148→  finally {
   149→    isSampleLoading.value = false
   150→  }
   151→}
   152→
   153→/**
   154→ * When the user switches document type from the header dropdown, load the
   155→ * sample XML for the newly selected type so there's always a valid document
   156→ * to preview. Only fires on explicit user action (not on initial page load).
   157→ */

    45→  name: 'PreviewPanel',
    46→})
    47→
    48→/**
    49→ * PreviewPanel Component
    50→ *
    51→ * Integration point combining XML parser (MVP 2) and template system (MVP 3).
    52→ * Provides real-time preview of XML content with error handling and zoom support.
    53→ *
    54→ * Props:
    55→ * - xmlContent: XML string to parse and render
    56→ * - zoom: Zoom level for scaling (default: 1, range: 0.75 - 1.5)
    57→ */
    58→
    59→interface Props {
    60→  xmlContent: string
    61→  zoom?: number
    62→}
    63→
    64→const props = withDefaults(defineProps<Props>(), {
    65→  zoom: 1,
    66→})
    67→
    68→// Reactive state
    69→const parsedData = ref<ParsedData | undefined>(undefined)
    70→const error = ref<string | undefined>(undefined)
    71→const isLoading = ref(false)
    72→
    73→// Get composables
    74→const { currentTemplate: templateComponent, activeTemplate } = useTemplate()
    75→const { currentDocumentType, activeDocumentType } = useDocumentType()
    76→
    77→// Computed style for zoom transform
    78→const containerStyle = computed(() => ({
    79→  transform: `scale(${props.zoom})`,
    80→  transformOrigin: 'top left',
    81→}))
    82→
    83→/**
    84→ * Parse XML and update component state
    85→ * Handles all parsing errors gracefully with user-friendly messages
    86→ */
    87→function updatePreview() {
    88→  isLoading.value = true
    89→  error.value = undefined
    90→  parsedData.value = undefined
    91→
    92→  try {
    93→    const parser = currentDocumentType.value?.parse
    94→    if (!parser) {
    95→      error.value = 'No parser available for the active document type'
    96→      isLoading.value = false
    97→      return
    98→    }
    99→
   100→    const result = parser(props.xmlContent)
   101→
   102→    if (result.success && result.data) {
   103→      parsedData.value = result.data
   104→      error.value = undefined
   105→    }
   106→    else {
   107→      error.value = result.error || 'Unknown parsing error occurred'
   108→      parsedData.value = undefined
   109→    }
   110→  }
   111→  catch (err) {
   112→    const errorMessage = err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Unknown error occurred'
   113→    error.value = `Preview error: ${errorMessage}`
   114→    parsedData.value = undefined
   115→  }
   116→  finally {
   117→    isLoading.value = false
   118→  }
   119→}
   120→
   121→// Re-parse when xmlContent, active template, or active document type changes
   122→watch(
   123→  [() => props.xmlContent, activeTemplate, activeDocumentType],
   124→  () => {
   125→    updatePreview()
   126→  },
   127→  { immediate: true },
   128→)
   129→</script>

Please provide valid XML content.',\n    }\n  }\n\n  const parser = new DOMParser()\n  const doc = parser.parseFromString(xmlString, 'text/xml')\n\n  const parserError = doc.querySelector('parsererror')\n  if (parserError) {\n    const errorText = parserError.textContent || 'Unknown XML parsing error'\n\n    if (errorText.includes('unclosed tag') || errorText.includes('Opening and ending tag mismatch')) {\n      return {\n        isValid: false,\n        error: 'XML has unclosed or mismatched tags. Please check that all opening tags have corresponding closing tags.',\n      }\n    }\n    if (errorText.includes('Unexpected end of file') || errorText.includes('premature end of data')) {\n      return {\n        isValid: false,\n        error: 'XML is incomplete. The document appears to end unexpectedly.',\n      }\n    }\n\n    return {\n      isValid: false,\n      error: `XML parsing error: ${errorText}`,\n    }\n  }\n\n  const root = doc.documentElement\n  if (!root || root.tagName !== 'resignationLetter') {\n    return {\n      isValid: false,\n      error: 'Invalid XML structure. Root element must be <resignationLetter>.',\n    }\n  }\n\n  const required = ['sender', 'date', 'recipient', 'body', 'signature']\n  for (const el of required) {\n    if (!root.querySelector(el)) {\n      return {\n        isValid: false,\n        error: `Missing required element: <${el}>. Resignation letters must include sender, date, recipient, body, and signature.`,\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  return { isValid: true }\n}\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500 Parse \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\nexport function parseResignationXml(xmlString: string): ParseResult {\n  try {\n    const validation = validateResignationXml(xmlString)\n    if (!validation.isValid) {\n      return { success: false, error: validation.error }\n    }\n\n    const parser = new DOMParser()\n    const doc = parser.parseFromString(xmlString, 'text/xml')\n    const root = doc.documentElement\n\n    const senderEl = root.querySelector('sender')\n    const recipientEl = root.querySelector('recipient')\n    const bodyEl = root.querySelector('body')\n    const signatureEl = root.querySelector('signature')\n\n    const sender: ResignationSender = {\n      name: getText(senderEl, 'name'),\n      position: getText(senderEl, 'position'),\n    }\n\n    const recipient: ResignationRecipient = {\n      name: getText(recipientEl, 'name'),\n      title: getText(recipientEl, 'title'),\n      company: getText(recipientEl, 'company'),\n    }\n\n    const body: string[] = bodyEl\n      ? Array.from(bodyEl.querySelectorAll('paragraph')).map(p => p.textContent?.trim() ?? '').filter(t => t)\n      : []\n\n    const signature: ResignationSignature = {\n      name: getText(signatureEl, 'name'),\n      position: getText(signatureEl, 'position'),\n    }\n\n    const data: ResignationParsedData = {\n      sender,\n      date: root.querySelector('date')?.textContent?.trim() ?? '',\n      recipient,\n      body,\n      signature,\n    }\n\n    return { success: true, data }\n  }\n  catch (error) {\n    const msg = error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error occurred during parsing'\n    return { success: false, error: `Failed to parse XML: ${msg}` }\n  }\n}\n"
